					30 03 1791 0:00:00		"The United States created an unnamed district (now the District of Columbia) to be the seat of the federal government. It was created from FAIRFAX, MONTGOMERY (Md.), and PRINCE GEORGES (Md.). The district was a square with each corner at a point of the compass (north, east, south, and west) with each side ten miles long. Until 27 February 1801, when Congress created two county in the district to provide local government in the district, the laws and county jurisdictions of Maryland and Virginia continued in the ceded areas."
